  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f141ebd7-7db3-4106-a90a-5f5d71bd7052'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer14971551761307050954">How it all started…<br/><br/>One day I was a high school teacher on summer break, leading a relatively uneventful but happy life. Or so I told myself. Later, I’d question that, as I would question pretty much everything I knew about me, my relationships, and my desires. It all began when my neighbor thrust a key to a storage unit at me. She’d bought it to make extra money after watc</span>
  <span id="freeText14971551761307050954" style="display:none">How it all started…<br /><br />One day I was a high school teacher on summer break, leading a relatively uneventful but happy life. Or so I told myself. Later, I’d question that, as I would question pretty much everything I knew about me, my relationships, and my desires. It all began when my neighbor thrust a key to a storage unit at me. She’d bought it to make extra money after watching some storage auction show. Now she was on her way to the airport to elope with a man she barely knew, and she needed me to clear out the unit before the lease expired.<br /><br />Soon, I was standing inside a small room that held the intimate details of another woman’s life, feeling uncomfortable, as if I was invading her privacy. Why had she let these items so neatly packed, possessions that she clearly cared about deeply, be lost at an auction? Driven to find out by some unnamed force, I began to dig, to discover this woman’s life, and yes, read her journals—-dark, erotic journals that I had no business reading. Once I started, I couldn’t stop. I read on obsessively, living out fantasies through her words that I’d never dare experience on my own, compelled by the three men in her life, none of whom had names. I read onward until the last terrifying dark entry left me certain that something had happened to this woman. I had to find her and be sure she was okay.<br /><br />Before long, I was taking her job for the summer at the art gallery, living her life, and she was nowhere to be found. I was becoming someone I didn’t know. I was becoming her.<br /><br />The dark, passion it becomes…<br /><br />Now, I am working at a prestigious gallery, where I have always dreamed of being, and I’ve been delivered to the doorstep of several men, all of which I envision as one I’ve read about in the journal. But there is one man that will call to me, that will awaken me in ways I never believed possible. That man is the ruggedly sexy artist, Chris Merit, who wants to paint me. He is rich and famous, and dark in ways I shouldn’t find intriguing, but I do. I so do. I don’t understand why his dark side appeals to me, but the attraction between us is rich with velvety promises of satisfaction. Chris is dark, and so are his desires, but I cannot turn away. He is damaged beneath his confident good looks and need for control, and in some way, I feel he needs me. I need him.<br /><br />All I know for certain is that he knows me like I don’t even know me, and he says I know him. Still, I keep asking myself — do I know him? Did he know her, the journal writer, and where is she? And why doesn’t it seem to matter anymore? There is just him and me, and the burn for more.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14971551761307050954" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>

    <div id=buyButtonContainer class="uitext buttons buyableFeature u-marginTopXSmall u-paddingBottomXSmall u-bottomGrayBorder" data-book-id=15717721 >

    <div class="u-positionRelative">

<div id="review_373500287" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/373500287" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/373500287?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to ~ Becs ~ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/3820197-jill">Jill</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=net-galley-for-review">net-galley-for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=review-copy">review-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=super-rich-hero">super-rich-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tattooed-hero">tattooed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer373500287" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16751337479435361839"><b>5 big shiny stars</b><br/><br/>I’ve read a lot of good books lately and only given them 4 stars. To give a book 5 stars, it’s got to totally consume me, to get deep under my skin and this book definitely did that. I need to feel the intensity of the character’s passion, the ferocity of their feelings and the depths of their despair and it’s all here in this book. It owned me. It would be easy just to sit here and rain down superlatives but I’ll try to be more constructive.<br/><br/>The problem with picking up the first</span>
  <span id="freeText16751337479435361839" style="display:none"><b>5 big shiny stars</b><br /><br />I’ve read a lot of good books lately and only given them 4 stars. To give a book 5 stars, it’s got to totally consume me, to get deep under my skin and this book definitely did that. I need to feel the intensity of the character’s passion, the ferocity of their feelings and the depths of their despair and it’s all here in this book. It owned me. It would be easy just to sit here and rain down superlatives but I’ll try to be more constructive.<br /><br />The problem with picking up the first of a trilogy is that you know, if the book is good, that you’re going to be left with questions unanswered and find yourself desperate for more. The book is good. I am desperate for more. All that remains is to wait patiently for the next book and patience is a very overrated virtue.<br /><br />This book is marketed as Fifty Shades of Grey meets Basic Instinct. I definitely see the 50 shades analogy and its similarity to Bared to You but I can’t see the Basic Instinct comparisons yet although I guess they may come in the final novels. Fifty Shades gets such a bad rap among reviewers these days, I really don’t want to put anyone off – this is really very good and it’s a different story and I was enthralled by it from beginning to end so don’t let that comparison put you off. Please give it a chance.<br /><br />The book is written in the first person POV and in the present tense. It’s the style used in 50 Shades and I was at first a little unsettled by this but it didn’t last long and I was soon sucked and the words sailed past as I got absorbed in the story. It actually worked well to differentiate between what is happening now and what has happened in the past as revealed by Rebecca’s journal entries.<br /><br />So, Sara, a school teacher, has found some journals and other items belonging to an Art gallery manager called Rebecca which contains vivid descriptions of her dazzling yet destructive affair with a dominant and controlling man. They’re highly emotive and erotic and Sara decides she must return them to Rebecca. She goes to the art gallery where she works but Rebecca is AWOL and the owner, Mark, offers her a summer job replacing Rebecca after he sees her interacting with prospective clients at the gallery. Sara is an arts graduate and it has always been her ambition to work in the arts field but is she now living Rebecca’s life?<br /><br />Mark, her new boss, is controlling and dominant and Sara feels sure he is the man Rebecca has written about in the journals. She meets Chris Merit, an artist she has admired for years, and their attraction is instant. Quite clearly, Mark and Chris can barely tolerate one another and Chris begins to behave highly territorially towards Sara around Mark. She eventually embarks on a passionate affair with Chris and they certainly set the pages aflame with their first encounter in Christ’s apartment. It was smoking hot!<br /><br />Most of this instalment of the trilogy is given over to the amazingly passionate relationship that develops between Chris and Sara. They’re both from highly privileged backgrounds and both feel damaged by this and agree that their relationship is just sex and nothing more and agree not to discuss their pasts but the intensity of their feelings shocks them both. Chris’s feelings for Sara are threatening his control and that’s not something he wants to give up easily. Sara is teetering on the edge of indecision – she’s taken aback by the intensity of their affair but not 100% sure she can trust him.<br /><br />Their relationship, certainly in the second half of their book, eclipses Rebecca’s storyline but it’s an underlying theme. Where is Rebecca? Who is the unnamed man in her journals? Who is the man watching Sara at Rebecca’s lockup?<br /><br />We’re left with a truly WICKED cliffhanger which has left me salivating for the next instalment in this trilogy. I can’t wait. Lisa – WRITE FASTER!!<br /><br />So, please don’t be put off by the Fifty Shades comparisons – this book is its own story. If you like deeply passionate love stories, darkly enigmatic heroes and an intriguing mystery then you should give this book a go.<br /><br />Thanks go to Jill for the awesome rec!<br /><br />For more of my reviews, please visit my <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Blog</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16751337479435361839" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_401185817" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/401185817" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/401185817?book_show_action=true">Aug 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=romantica-or-erotica">romantica-or-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=super-cheese">super-cheese</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=frustrating">frustrating</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=bdsm-or-person-in-control">bdsm-or-person-in-control</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=suspense-or-thriller">suspense-or-thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer401185817" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4313113262361417359"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Something has happened to Rebecca, and I have to prove it. That's why I'm here. No other reason.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>That's right, girl. Stick to your guns. Or not. Well, at least you lasted a day or two before you cracked. Way to stay strong.<br/><br/><b>I almost didn't read this book. The summary blurb <i>really</i> made me not want to read this book.</b><br/><br/><b>2.5 stars.</b> What is it with everyone these days trying to sell their book as the "next" something? Whether it's the next Harry Potter, the next Hunger Games, etc. Everybody se</span>
  <span id="freeText4313113262361417359" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>Something has happened to Rebecca, and I have to prove it. That's why I'm here. No other reason.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>That's right, girl. Stick to your guns. Or not. Well, at least you lasted a day or two before you cracked. Way to stay strong.<br><br><b>I almost didn't read this book. The summary blurb <i>really</i> made me not want to read this book.</b><br><br><b>2.5 stars.</b> What is it with everyone these days trying to sell their book as the "next" something? Whether it's the next Harry Potter, the next Hunger Games, etc. Everybody seems to want to cash in on being the next big thing by being the next version of the last big thing. Here's the problem I have with this : <i>if the book is TOO much like the book it's being compared to, it's going to be game over for me.</i> I don't want to read a copy of another book, especially if it's going to read like <i>fanfiction of <u>another</u> fanfiction (in case you're the last person on the planet to know this, Fifty was fanfiction).</i> Then on the other side : <i>if the book is NOTHING like the book it's being compared to, then I'm going to wonder why the book was compared in the first place.</i><br><br>So, either way, this comparison strategy is something I'm not a fan of. I didn't intially want to read this because it's yet another book being compared to Fifty. Been there, done that, don't really want to be sucked into reading another copy of Fifty again. Yet, here we are. I requested the galley out of morbid curiosity, my friends were reading it, and I said, "aw hell, let's do this..." Yes, I am that easy.<br><br><i>Light spoilers ahead. No big reveals, but I will be talking about a few plot issues.</i><br><br><b>The mystery element is what had me curious.</b> I've read my fair share of erotic books (don't ask to see my GR erotic account, you'll be terrified at some of my bizarre choices), yet I don't seem to recall reading anything that tried to sell itself as a mystery within an erotica. It's too bad that the mystery took a backseat to the Chris and Sara drama. First off, I had a hard time understanding why Sara took such an interest in what happened to Rebecca. There wasn't any huge indicator that something horrible had happened. A lot of what she was thinking was a guess. But okay, fine...we'll go with the fact that Sara was so intrigued by the mystery of Rebecca that she not only had the desire, but also the time (so convenient that she happened to be a schoolteacher off for the summer) to go play amateur detective. <br><br>Unfortunately, there wasn't much digging going on. I guess that's what happens when a hot guy gets in the way and wants to get you naked. <i>All of your plans go right out the window.</i> Now, I can't say that I wouldn't do the same thing in a similar situation, because hot guy plus hot sex is probably more fun than chasing slivers of evidence around. <br><br>BUT...here's where the Fifty nonsense comes in...<i>she let hot guy push her around, even when she didn't want him to (at least that's what we were hearing in her head - how much she didn't want to give up her control).</i> Can I just say that this must go far beyond grade-A "best sex of your life" sex if after one night, you're letting someone else win the power struggle. Maybe if this had been a dom/sub situation left in the bedroom, it would have been okay. <i>But it wasn't.</i> This was "hey girl, you think you're going to make a decision and I'm going to override you," type of stuff. Never mind that Sara has no <i>clue</i> who the possible culprit in a possible crime is. Obviously, she wasn't suspecting Chris (that was left up to us as the reader to speculate), but since she knows he has ties to the guy who she IS suspecting, she probably should have considered any tie to be a lead.<br><br><b>When faced the with the decision to get to know someone who has ties to a potential criminal, you can either :</b><br><br>1. Get naked for the hot artist guy who has control issues.<br><br>2. Spend more time getting to know him in a very public setting, before deciding whether or not he is trustworthy. Preferably in a place with cameras, just in case you find out something awkward.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389144i/750144.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh wait, but there were cameras. Who knew? Our upstanding man Chris tried to get naughty with Sara in front of some cameras (which she didn't know about) in order to send a message to another male in competition for Sara. You know, the message of the "back off" kind. OH HAI THERE <s>Fifty</s> uh <s>Knight</s> uh Chris. You're a gem. It's so nice to meet a guy who thinks he can claim his prize when he's not even officially with the girl yet. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Are you one of those dark, messed up, arrogant assholes?"<br>"I'm worse."</i>
    <b></b>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Girl, he's been telling you all along that he's bad news. I get being intrigued by the "dangerous" guy, but you have lost all of your brain cells for not proceeding with at least a little more caution. In another scene he said, "losing control and you taking it from me are two different things. You won't ever take it from me." That right there is a cautionary red flag in my book. The fact that she refers to Chris as her "poor damaged artist" after spending next to no time with him is mind boggling. I half expected her to call him Fifty Shades of Fucked up. <br><br><b>So what else ruffled my imaginary feathers?</b><br><br>Oh, the usual suspects. References to a person being like a drug addiction and the lovely nickname baby. Because the first 100 times I've seen it before in other books weren't enough. Yay!<br><br><b>Come on, you say...there had to be something good, right?</b><br><br>There was! Chris was not perfect (aside from the obvious "might be a killer" and stalking aspects). I thought it was awesome that he couldn't cook. I love me some men who can cook, but at least this guy had a flaw outside of being wealthy, artistic and hot as an exploding firecracker.<br><br>I also did like that there was a mystery element. As stated earlier, I wish there had been <i>more</i> to this, but I did find myself coming up with a few semi-lame theories. Without the mystery element, this would be an extremely weak erotic story with no strong plot to carry anything.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Maybe he's right. Maybe I am playing with fire, but I cannot stop myself. Beyond reason, I will push him until he reveals everything.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Yep. And that's why I'm going to read book 2. Because pushing might escalate into shoving. Personally, I hope someone goes psycho killer on everyone's ass, but I know it's just wishful thinking on my part.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>But this isn't supposed to be about me. Rebecca. Remember how this all started.<i></i></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Hopefully, in the next book she'll remember to follow through on this.<br><br><i>This book was provided from the publisher through Netgalley in exchange for an honest review. <br><br><br><br><br><br> <br></i></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer646367723" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer378332861668465849">This is a book that I've seen around for a long time. I've wanted to read it, but never got around to it until now. I have to say that it was worth the wait. This story has completely monopolized my thoughts since I started this series.<br/><br/>Part romance, part mystery, 'If I Were You' tells the story of a schoolteacher turned investigator by chance. When Sara's best friend, Ella, gifts her the contents of a storage unit that she purchased at an auction, Sara becomes obsessed with finding out what happ</span>
  <span id="freeText378332861668465849" style="display:none">This is a book that I've seen around for a long time. I've wanted to read it, but never got around to it until now. I have to say that it was worth the wait. This story has completely monopolized my thoughts since I started this series.<br /><br />Part romance, part mystery, 'If I Were You' tells the story of a schoolteacher turned investigator by chance. When Sara's best friend, Ella, gifts her the contents of a storage unit that she purchased at an auction, Sara becomes obsessed with finding out what happened to the original owner of the belongings. <br /><br />Amongst the belongings, are the personal journals of a woman named Rebecca. She pours her heart out in her journals, revealing her most private desires and chronicling her sexual interactions with an unnamed man she referred to as her master. It is clear that Rebecca came to dread the sexual games she shared with this man and decided to leave him. Then, the trail goes cold.<br /><br />When Sara decides to try and track Rebecca down to return her belongings, she soon finds herself stepping into her shoes. Sara is hired by the domineering Mark to fill in for Rebecca at the art gallery where she worked. While trying to navigate this new and intimidating world of the wealthy elite, Sara begins to question whether or not Rebecca has fallen into harms way and who might be involved.<br /><br />Sara also begins a sexual relationship with the famous artist, Chris Merit. From the start, he makes it clear that he isn't the "happily ever after" type of guy. However, the two grow inexplicably closer and soon boundaries are crossed. Despite the fact that they're both keeping secrets, they cannot seem to stay away from each other.<br /><br />I thoroughly enjoyed this suspenseful story. I'm dying to know what happened to Rebecca and who was involved. This story kept me guessing the entire time. It keeps you hanging, so I'll be continuing the series immediately. The upside of waiting so long is that I won't have to wait for the next book to be released.</span>

<div id="review_354204781" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/354204781" />
    <a title="Lisa Jones" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1892928-lisa-jones"><img alt="Lisa Jones" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1606190659p2/1892928.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/354204781?book_show_action=true">Jun 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa Jones" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa Jones" href="/user/show/1892928-lisa-jones">Lisa Jones</a>

          added it


          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span> (Review from the author)

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer354204781" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3422419424657416952"><strong>I'm returning to the Inside Out world with Riptide and Mark Compton in a new seductive erotic mystery: THE BRILLIANCE TRILOGY!</strong> Readers will be able to read this series without having read the Inside Out series, but if you've missed Mark, Chris, and Sara, you will be seeing a lot of them in this trilogy!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1588138211i/29374202._SX540_.jpg' alt='' width='400' height='218' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><strong>ABOUT BOOK ONE</strong><br/>It all started with a note, just a simple note hand written by a woman I didn't know, never even met. But in that note is perhaps every answer to every question I've ever had in my l</span>
  <span id="freeText3422419424657416952" style="display:none"><strong>I'm returning to the Inside Out world with Riptide and Mark Compton in a new seductive erotic mystery: THE BRILLIANCE TRILOGY!</strong> Readers will be able to read this series without having read the Inside Out series, but if you've missed Mark, Chris, and Sara, you will be seeing a lot of them in this trilogy!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1588138211i/29374202._SX540_.jpg" alt="" width="400" height="218" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><strong>ABOUT BOOK ONE</strong><br>It all started with a note, just a simple note hand written by a woman I didn't know, never even met. But in that note is perhaps every answer to every question I've ever had in my life. And because of that note, I travel thousands of miles. I look for her, but find him. I'm drawn to his passion, his talent, a darkness in him that somehow becomes my light, my life. I know he has secrets. I don't care. Because you see, I have secrets, too.<br><br>I’m not Aria Alard, daughter to an Italian musician, as he believes. I’m Aria Stradivari, daughter to Alessandro Stradivari, a musician born from the same blood as the man who created the famous Stradivari violin. I am as rare as the mere 650 instruments my ancestors created. Instruments worth millions. 650 masterpieces, the brilliance unmatched. 650 reasons to kill. 650 reasons to hide. One reason to not to: him.<br><br><strong>BUY A RECKLESS NOTE (book one)</strong><br>Amazon → <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://mybook.to/RecklessNote">http://mybook.to/RecklessNote</a><br>Apple → <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://apple.co/37kJZMH">https://apple.co/37kJZMH</a><br>Nook → <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://bit.ly/2sSxFnU">https://bit.ly/2sSxFnU</a><br>Kobo → <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://bit.ly/30KXC54">https://bit.ly/30KXC54</a><br><br><strong>PRE-ORDER THE REST OF THE SERIES → <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://bit.ly/2SdujFA">https://bit.ly/2SdujFA</a></strong><br><br><strong>LIMITED EDITION TOTE BAGS &amp; SIGNED BOOKS</strong><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1588138211i/29374201._SY540_.jpg" alt="" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I have a very limited stock of these amazing Brilliance Trilogy tote bags! You can buy one by itself, or along with a personalized signed copy of A Reckless Note!<br>Check them out here → <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://bit.ly/2KD82wm">https://bit.ly/2KD82wm</a></span>

<div id="review_390703214" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/390703214" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/390703214?book_show_action=true">Aug 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940015194197" href="/book/show/15717728-if-i-were-you">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer390703214" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8575246509456669554"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380387490i/747518._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>GAH!!!! <b> NONE OF MY QUESTIONS WERE ANSWERED!!!! </b> and I literally mean <i> <b> none </b></i>  of them *lip quiver*<br/><br/>I feel a little cheated... I mean, it was a really good book - it totally hooked me into the story, made me care about the characters, got me all hot and bothered, and filled my mind with approximately 4 bajillion questions and theories and then... <i> <b> left me hanging!!! </b></i> <br/><br/>O_O <br/><br/>I don't really know what to say. I feel like I know about as much now as I did at the beginning of the book :| <br/><br/><blockquote> <i> <b> "People aren</b></i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText8575246509456669554" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380387490i/747518._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>GAH!!!! <b> NONE OF MY QUESTIONS WERE ANSWERED!!!! </b> and I literally mean <i> <b> none </b></i>  of them *lip quiver*<br><br>I feel a little cheated... I mean, it was a really good book - it totally hooked me into the story, made me care about the characters, got me all hot and bothered, and filled my mind with approximately 4 bajillion questions and theories and then... <i> <b> left me hanging!!! </b></i> <br><br>O_O <br><br>I don't really know what to say. I feel like I know about as much now as I did at the beginning of the book :| <br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> "People arent always what they seem...The art does not always mimic the artist. You never know the real person until you slide beneath their surface." </b></i>  </blockquote><br><br>The story follows Sara, a high school teacher whose passion in life is art and ends up getting possession of a storage locker that belongs to a mystery woman named Rebecca, whose journals Sara finds and reads. The journals are erotic and mysterious telling the story of Rebecca's spiral into a relationship with a dangerously sexy and controlling Dom.<br><br>The story is addictive - draws you RIGHT in. Its a deliciously thrilling and dangerously erotic mystery with a dual storyline going on between the current day life of Sara and the life of Rebecca as read in her journals.<br><br>These are the beginning lines of the book:<br><br><blockquote>
<i> "Dangerous.<br>For months I've had dreams and nightmares about how perfectly he personifies the word. Sleep-laden, alternate realities where I can vividly smell hi musky male scent, feel his hard body against mine. Taste the sweet and sensuous flavor of him -- like milk chocolate with its silky demands that I indulge in one more bite. And another. So good I'd forgotten there's a price for overindulgence. And there is a price.... It started out as any other erotic adventure with him. Unpredictable. Exciting. I barely remember how it all went wrong. How it took such a dark turn." </i> </blockquote><br><br>See what I mean? You kinda just <i> need </i> to know more!<br><br>The more Sara discovers about Rebecca, the deeper and darker the mystery gets. New journal entries lead to more questions which in turn lead to a plethora of possibilities.<br><br>Since the last journal entry was rather ominous, Sara decides to try and find Rebecca, but, having no idea where to start, she goes to the art gallery where Rebecca worked as a starting point. There she meets the gallery manager, Mark Compton, who is sophisticated, powerful, controlling, arrogant, and alluringly sexy who offers her Rebecca's job while she is 'away'. On the same day, Sara also meets one of the famous artists whose work is displayed at the gallery, Chris Merit - he's a rebel, tattooed, doesn't play by the rules, gorgeous, raw, mysterious and with a dark side that he keeps trying to warn her away from. Drawn to him and intrigued by the gallery manager, Sara slips deeper and deeper into Rebecca's world. And the more she is drawn into the mystery of unraveling Rebecca's life, the more her own life starts to entwine with hers.<br><br>This book was HOT - those journal entries were scorching!! I can see how some people have compared it to Fifty Shades. I wouldn't compare it personally, but it definitely had Fifty-ish vibes in certain places but the story stands completely alone. The relationship that Rebecca talks about in the journals is a BDSM one with some mystery guy. We can suspect who he is, but honestly the evidence could point in any number of directions so we don't really know.<br><br>And the heroine made some choices and decisions along the way that I didn't fully see as being understandable, so that did disconnect me here and there from the story a little, but I just tried to be understanding and so it wasn't a huge deal but I still did go 'hmmmm' a few times... for example: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ 1) When her best friend elopes suddenly with two hours warning and goes off to Paris on a honeymoon with a man she has never met and then she doens't hear from her for over a week except for one garbled phone call, personally, I'd be worried, but she didn't seem to think anything of it :S ... 2) I never understood why she would read bits of the journal here and there. If she was so interested in finding Rebecca, why wouldn't she read every work cover to cover right off the bat? ...and finally, 3) I didn't really like how she would get so upset with Chris over pretty much everything.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I totally loved the hero (or, rather, one of them? again, I'm not really sure). He had that delicious flawed aspect with just the right amount of mystery to him to make me love him and yet wonder about him.<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> "Be warned, Sara. I'm no saint. If I take you upstairs, I'm going to strip you naked and fuck you the way I've wanted to since the moment we first met." </b></i>  </blockquote><br><br>The ending is a HUGE <i> <b> cliffhanger </b> </i>. Literally the story just stops at an "omg" moment... I will say that I've never been fond of cliffhangers and I think I would have been more fine with this one had I had a few more questions answered (or any for that matter). Either way *sigh* yes, I will totally be going on to book 2.... <b> I NEED TO KNOW WHAT HAPPENS!!!!!! </b><br><br>I have a feeling that when all three books are out, these may end up on my favorites list, but for now, I'm just a frustrated mess... <br><br>*runs off to find herself a guaranteed HEA book* <br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="8575246509456669554" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer408050708" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18026472911385637014">ALL I HAVE TO SAY IS 20-FREAKING-13??? THAT SHOULD BE ILLEGAL! <br/><br/>If you are my friend it is a prerequisite that you tell me when there is a cliffhanger – I mean a real cliffhanger with no closure and I have to wait 5 flipping months to find out what the heck happens next! GAH!<br/><br/>Okay, now that I have my tantrum out of the way I can honestly say IF I WERE YOU was amazing – yes, AMAZING! For all of you who may be avoiding this book because of the FIFTY SHADES OF GREY reference in the book's description</span>
  <span id="freeText18026472911385637014" style="display:none">ALL I HAVE TO SAY IS 20-FREAKING-13??? THAT SHOULD BE ILLEGAL! <br /><br />If you are my friend it is a prerequisite that you tell me when there is a cliffhanger – I mean a real cliffhanger with no closure and I have to wait 5 flipping months to find out what the heck happens next! GAH!<br /><br />Okay, now that I have my tantrum out of the way I can honestly say IF I WERE YOU was amazing – yes, AMAZING! For all of you who may be avoiding this book because of the FIFTY SHADES OF GREY reference in the book's description, just get that out of your head right now because there really are very few similarities. Well, yes, there is a heroine who is innocent to the world of BDSM and is intrigued by the thought of it. Yes, there is a hot hero who is wealthy and has a big secret, but that’s where I think it ends. Lovers of “FIFTY” will love it and the critics of “FIFTY” who love romantic suspense with BDSM undertones will love it. <br /><br />Meet the mysterious cast of characters:<br /><br />Rebecca Mason is the missing gallery salesperson and author of the erotic journal that initially intrigues Sara about the world of BDSM. <br /><br />Sara McMillan is high school teacher by trade who is also somewhat of an art expert finds herself in “Wonderland” also known as the Allure Art Gallery in a quest to uncover answers to the perplexing disappearance of the journal’s owner, Rebecca. In a fantastic twist of fate, Sara acquires a job at the prestigious gallery, affording her the opportunity to get to know more about Rebecca and her life. As the story unfolds, Sara becomes cognizant of the fact that nothing is as it appears. It seems that everyone she encounters who knew Rebecca adds another level of complexity to her new life and further complicates what was started as a simple inquisition has now turned into something else all together. <br /><br />Mark Compton, sexy gallery owner and über dominant…don’t worry, I’m not giving anything away, because this fact is glaringly obvious from the get-go. There is not much else I can tell you except for he is as enigmatic, if not more so than any of the characters.<br /><br />Chris Merit. Oh boy, Chris Merit…I love him. I loathe him. No, I really love him, but I hate his mood swings, but that is what makes him interesting and real. The accomplished artist is confidently controlled when it comes to just about everything…everything except for Sara. He sets his sights on her right away and his dark and brooding persona draws her into his web.<br /><br />I am not happy at all about the serious cliffhanger, but I am only mad because I am dying to know what happens next. If you love a good mystery that is sexy and exciting, then you have to read this first book in the INSIDE OUT trilogy, IF I WERE YOU – don’t be mad at me when you love it because I warned you the next book isn’t out until <s>February</s> JUNE 2013. Lisa Renee Jones, I beg you to write faster!<br /><br /><br />✳✳ Reviewed on <a href="http://bookienookiereviews.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">I ♥ Bookie Nookie Reviews</a><br /><br /><br />___________________________________________________<br />If you like this type of book, you might enjoy one of these groups. <div id="review_374127553" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/374127553" />
    <a title="KatLynne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2435483-katlynne"><img alt="KatLynne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1296698899p2/2435483.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/374127553?book_show_action=true">Jul 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="KatLynne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="KatLynne" href="/user/show/2435483-katlynne">KatLynne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Nook 2940015194197" href="/book/show/15717728-if-i-were-you">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to KatLynne by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/3820197-jill">Jill</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=2012-reads">2012-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=favorite-treasures">favorite-treasures</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=g-erotic-romance">g-erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=hero-hottie-billionaire">hero-hottie-billionaire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=tattooed-bad-boy-hottie">tattooed-bad-boy-hottie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=hero-dark-brooding">hero-dark-brooding</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=hero-favorite-smokin-hot-sexay">hero-favorite-smokin-hot-sexay</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=heroine-with-backbone-smart-strong">heroine-with-backbone-smart-strong</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2435483-katlynne?shelf=keeper">keeper</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer374127553" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15428440997608831841"><b>5 Big Stars</b><br/><br/>Lisa Renee Jones' <i>If I Were You</i> is the first book in <i>The Inside Out Trilogy.</i> I found it to be extremely suspenseful and captivating, while giving me an incredibly seductive, sexy read! I was enthralled from the very first page! <br/><br/>Sara McMillin is a high school teacher on summer break. Art is her true love, but she’s settled for a career that ensures a big enough pay check to make ends meet. Her life is pretty uneventful until her good friend and neighbor, Ella, thrust a key to an abando</span>
  <span id="freeText15428440997608831841" style="display:none"><b>5 Big Stars</b><br /><br />Lisa Renee Jones' <i>If I Were You</i> is the first book in <i>The Inside Out Trilogy.</i> I found it to be extremely suspenseful and captivating, while giving me an incredibly seductive, sexy read! I was enthralled from the very first page! <br /><br />Sara McMillin is a high school teacher on summer break. Art is her true love, but she’s settled for a career that ensures a big enough pay check to make ends meet. Her life is pretty uneventful until her good friend and neighbor, Ella, thrust a key to an abandoned storage unit into her hands and ask her to dispose of the contents. It strikes Sara as odd that anyone would go to the trouble of packing all their possessions away with such care and then completely abandon them. Driven to find this missing woman, Sara becomes absorbed in Rebecca Mason’s dark, erotic journals. They are mesmerizing, filled with Rebecca’s thoughts, her feelings and fears concerning the man or <i>men</i> in her life.<blockquote>Seeking answers, Sara visits the prestigious Art Galley where Rebecca worked. A situation arises and she is given a chance to walk into the world she’d only dreamed about. Taking a summer position leaves Sara feeling alive for the first time in years. I quickly learn Sara is smart, knows her subject matter well and has the kind of backbone I admire in a heroine. Also, there seems to be skeletons in her closet and somewhere in her past she was once broken. </blockquote>This is my first book by this author and it won't be my last. Ms. Jones took me on a journey that is gripping, sensual, and one of the best I’ve read this year. There is secrecy surrounding every aspect of the story, keeping me in suspense and questioning the motives of every man I met. Was the man in Rebecca’s journals Sara’s new boss at the Art Gallery, the sexy, controlling and magnetic Mark Compton? He’s rich, powerful and has the classic good looks women are drawn to. There’s also something raw and sexual about him, almost a predatory feeling. Without a doubt he has that “animal magnetism” that Rebecca referred to in her journals.<br /><br />And what about Chris Merit! This very talented man is dripping sexual charisma. "Unlike Mark, he is not classically good looking, but more raw male hotness." While he is utterly divine, he’s also dark, damaged and surrounded by mystery. <br /><br />The chemistry between Sara and Chris is explosive and soon we have two damaged people together, each struggling with their own ghost from their past and a relationship that is fragile and fraught with many unknown elements. The affair between these two develops rather quickly as they are drawn to each other like magnets. There are scorching hot love scenes with one in particular involving a huge window overlooking the Bay area. It is quite memorable! Just as quickly, the heart becomes involved and I wonder as they get to know each other better, will there be heartache ahead? <br /><br />The ending left me gasping and my head is full of questions. Who is this mystery man Rebecca wrote about in her journals? Is it one man or possibly more? Could it be someone I haven’t met? Is there a rich boyfriend? Or could it be one of the artists whose work is on display? Could it be Mark Compton, or Chris? Is she in danger or just away having the time of her life? <br /><br /><i>If I Were You</i> easily stands on its own merit. There are a few similarities to FSoG, but for me this one is so much better. One of the biggest things they share is the cliffhanger ending. While this is a brilliant marketing device, it’s very detrimental to my well being. I’m a very impatient reader. I want a finale, a finish, a conclusion at the end of a book. I am one of those readers who would have taken the great Charles Dickens’ weekly or monthly installments and saved them all until finished before I commenced reading:) <br /><br />Knowing this ends with a riveting cliffhanger, one that left me breathless, would I recommend reading this book now? <b>Absolutely!</b> I give it a full five stars due to the power this book had on me and my unwillingness to put it down. As the author fed me tidbits of information throughout, I needed more. Hopefully, the second or third installment will reveal my much sought out answers. <br /><br />I know I will read this one again. I also know I will run, jog, drive across town, or simply hit that “one click” button, doing whatever is necessary to ensure the next installment is in my hands the minute it is released. Yes, that's how anxious I am. I <b>must know</b> and I can hardly wait!<br /><br />Thank you to my GR friend, Jill, who recommended this to me! As I've said before, I covet your recs:)<br /><br />The expected release date is August 24, 2012 and I highly recommend this to all those who love a dark, sensual, hot romance surrounded by a mystery that is so intriguing that it easily vied for first place. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>Book 1: If I Were You - 5/5 Stars</i>
</b><br />Book 2: Being Me <br />Book 3: Revealing Us<br /><br />Thank you <i>Netgalley</i> and <i>Lisa Renee Jones</i> for the chance to read this early. It was awesome!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15428440997608831841" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/384063459?book_show_action=true">Aug 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer384063459" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5967775311098574336"><b>The next "it" book.</b><br/><br/>I'm pretty sure amazeballs just exploded amazejuices all over the pages! <br/><br/>At first I had a big OS moment, thinking I had been seduced by yet another synopsis. I just couldn't get into the first couple of chapters. But by chapter 5, <i>it</i> got into me. It got into me fast...hard! I'm so glad I didn't give up on this book.<br/><br/>I'm giving this book a standing "O" (it's only fair that I return the favor). OH! OH! OH. MY. GOD! I've been seduced by something dark, thrilling and totally addict</span>
  <span id="freeText5967775311098574336" style="display:none"><b>The next "it" book.</b><br /><br />I'm pretty sure amazeballs just exploded amazejuices all over the pages! <br /><br />At first I had a big OS moment, thinking I had been seduced by yet another synopsis. I just couldn't get into the first couple of chapters. But by chapter 5, <i>it</i> got into me. It got into me fast...hard! I'm so glad I didn't give up on this book.<br /><br />I'm giving this book a standing "O" (it's only fair that I return the favor). OH! OH! OH. MY. GOD! I've been seduced by something dark, thrilling and totally addictive! <br /><br />A few of the reviews suggest that this is a <i>Fifty Shades</i> mini-me (insert bullshit sneeze here). You can't say that every book that contains a little kinky fuckery is doing it <i>Fifty Shades</i> style! It had its own way of doing "it". The plot is totally <s>fuckable</s> original. <br /><br /><i>If I Were You</i> just barely scratches the surface of what I know is to come. It was word lubricant getting me primed and ready for something big, something huge!!! Something thrilling!<br /><br />You don't know if you want to scream, YES...NO...NOW! It blurs the line, seduces the soul, and leaves you begging for more! READ ON!<br /><br />Reviewed at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://toughcriticbookreviews.blogspot.com/">http://toughcriticbookreviews.blogspo...</a></span>

Its here where the book starts going through this unforeseen twists and turns that are enough to keep you turning the pages and gobbling it all up till you reach the very end . <br><br><u>THE SETTING</u> :<br>This book finds its base in San Francisco , amongst the rich and highly famous . Art , wine , fun and everything nice easily available to those who need it . <br><br><u> THE CHARACTERS </u> :<br><br>Saran McMillan : Sarah , like I mentioned earlier , is a school teacher who has given up on her dreams just to get her bills paid .. <i> her words , not mine </i> . Sarah as a character is someone who you could easily associalte with . She has dreams , aspirations to become something in the field of her interest , ART . An interest or passion that she had to give up on when life hit her hard and bad . On the surface she <i> at most of the time </i> appears to be someone calm , but in reality she is all but a whirlwind of emotions . She masks her fulfillement of dreams behind the 'I need to know what happened to Rebecca Mason' facade . Dont get me wrong , its not she's the bad guy here , but she's clever . She has an undying curiousity that makes her the target of all things dark and dangerous . Her thoughts merged with Rebecca's journal definitely had me thinking that I'm the one going through all stuffs happening in this book . <br><br>Chris Merit :<br><br>Ah yes , the famously infamous Chris Merit , painter/artist extraordinaire . No one is who they seem and everyone's keeping secrets they dare not talk about . With a cliffhanger enough to make you go insane , this one's a must read for me . <br><br>Highly Intense , Highly mysterious and awesomely sexy , If I were you is definitely the next 'IT' book that will leave you panting for more !!!! <br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/wink%20gif/JBeebziloveu/tumblr_lpai62DSqO1qbbtcs.gif?o=10" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer391707498" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1989376866916351931">This book. THIS BOOK!!! That's it. That's my review. I can't form coherent thought. All I can do is think of a ridiculous string of profanities that I want to yell while jumping up and down and running around in a circle waving my arms like wacky inflatable arm flailing tube man!<br/><br/><i>If I Were You</i> was effing amazing. AH-MAAAAAZING! I know there are people comparing it to <i>Fifty Shades</i> and I can see the similarities, what with all the HOT SEX, but really, this story is completely different and I loved </span>
  <span id="freeText1989376866916351931" style="display:none">This book. THIS BOOK!!! That's it. That's my review. I can't form coherent thought. All I can do is think of a ridiculous string of profanities that I want to yell while jumping up and down and running around in a circle waving my arms like wacky inflatable arm flailing tube man!<br><br><i>If I Were You</i> was effing amazing. AH-MAAAAAZING! I know there are people comparing it to <i>Fifty Shades</i> and I can see the similarities, what with all the HOT SEX, but really, this story is completely different and I loved every second of it. <br> <br>It's a slow build. Sara finds these amazingly erotic journals and is determined to find the woman they belong to and make sure she's okay. You will be right there with her, questioning and wondering who the dominating man in the journals is. But as the story progresses, she loses herself in this woman's world and gets caught up in the absolute pure, unadulterated sex that is Chris Merit. There are no words for this man. I love him, I love him and Sara together. Just LOVE! And believe me, you will get caught up right along with Sara. I tore through this book in one day. I just couldn't get enough. So much so that I completely lost track of the page count and then <b>BAM! </b>The story ends and I'm left trying to pick my jaw up off the floor wondering if that just happened. Did the author really just do that to me?!?!<br><br>This book is definitely cliffy! But oh it is so so soooooo worth it. A book hasn't gotten under my skin like this in a long time. I can't stop thinking about it. I might have to go back and read it again right away. But I have a feeling that this is only the beginning... <i>If I Were You</i> is just a preview of the awesomeness that is to come in this trilogy and I can NOT wait!!!<br><br><b>9/11/12 Edit</b><br><i>I just happened to come across this picture and all I could think of was ::sigh:: Chris Merit. YES, I'm <b>still</b> thinking about this book almost two weeks later! So here is my Chris Merit</i> &lt;3<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380744420i/3118339._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>More reviews at <a href="http://thebooklistreviews.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">thebooklistreviews.blogspot.com</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=trilogies">trilogies</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer401151031" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10236479577852908422"><b>4 Erotically Suspenseful Stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405458105i/10400144._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>Everything I do is calculated and with purpose. You'll learn that sooner of later.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405457059ra/10399987.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>If I had read this book when it first came out a couple years ago, it would have easily been 5 stars. Having had quite a few books in this genre under my belt, I can't say that it was an all encompassing 5 star read, but it was definitely a very strong 4 stars. I loved the combination of suspense, romance, and mystery here. I can tell you I was definitely hooked from the fi</span>
  <span id="freeText10236479577852908422" style="display:none"><b>4 Erotically Suspenseful Stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405458105i/10400144._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Everything I do is calculated and with purpose. You'll learn that sooner of later.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405457059ra/10399987.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>If I had read this book when it first came out a couple years ago, it would have easily been 5 stars. Having had quite a few books in this genre under my belt, I can't say that it was an all encompassing 5 star read, but it was definitely a very strong 4 stars. I loved the combination of suspense, romance, and mystery here. I can tell you I was definitely hooked from the first few pages.<br><br>It all starts with a diary...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405457059ra/10399988.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Art major at heart but high school teacher by day Sara leads an ordinary life...more or less. But then everything takes a dramatic turn with a few stolen glimpses of a very erotic journal. After her friend purchases a storage unit that has among its contents, journals. But these are not ordinary journals. These are the journals of one woman's erotically gripping journey with a man that equal parts terrifies and draws her to him like a magnet.<br><br>After reading page after page, Sara finds herself not only gripped by every word and experience of the journal's owner, Rebecca, but she feels compelled to find out what happened to her. She doesn't believe a woman would just dissapear and leave such personal items behind. Something must have happened to her, right?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405457059ra/10399989.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This is how she finds herself standing inside a gallery where Rebecca works and face to face with it's enigmatic owner, Mark. But it's another man entirely that captures her attention irrevocably; Chris Merit, playboy and renowned painter.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405457059i/10399990._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Within every wall lies a mystery and every word written and said brings questions. Sara soon begins to question everything as her life spirals more and more into a dark pleasure she has never before experienced.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405457059ra/10399991.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>She knows that Mark is hiding something, but what? And Chris is certainly not at all what he seems to be either.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404536077ra/10253583.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But will her quest for answers lead her to a danger that she doesn't see coming?<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405457059ra/10399992.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I definitely enjoyed this book, but it really left me with more questions than answers. I've very glad that I waited to read when all the books have been released, because that cliffy at the end would have made me stabby kind of angry. As it was, I'm very curious to see how it all ends and the secrets all revealed.<br><br>I was glad that Sara wasn't the typical virgin ingenue that I find in my books lately. Chris was the character that really stole the show for me. Still waters run deep with that one, and you can definitely tell that he hides some dark secrets and I for one can't wait to find out what they are. I was also very intrigued with Mark and the history that he so obviously has with Chris.<br><br>Jumping straight into book 2 now and hopefully getting some answers soon.<br><br><i>**ARC gifted to Dirty Girl Romance blog in exchange for an honest review**</i><br><br><b>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380436206i/881587.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10236479577852908422" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

<span id="freeTextContainer6312025969217589586"><i> If I Were You</i> for me is a book that <b>pretends to be something it is not</b>, it pretends to have a wow factor, when in actuality it doesn't have it. <br/><br/>There are many places where this book when wrong for me:<br/><br/>-	I didn't like the female main character, I found her incoherent and painstakingly easily manipulated. <br/><br/>-	<b>The story dragged</b> for me, so I started to lose interest and it became a little tedious. <br/><br/>-	There is <b>no real advance in the plot, is somewhat static, contradictory and deceitful</b> as it might look </span>
  <span id="freeText6312025969217589586" style="display:none"><i> If I Were You</i> for me is a book that <b>pretends to be something it is not</b>, it pretends to have a wow factor, when in actuality it doesn't have it. <br /><br />There are many places where this book when wrong for me:<br /><br />-	I didn't like the female main character, I found her incoherent and painstakingly easily manipulated. <br /><br />-	<b>The story dragged</b> for me, so I started to lose interest and it became a little tedious. <br /><br />-	There is <b>no real advance in the plot, is somewhat static, contradictory and deceitful</b> as it might look like the story is progressing when it really isn't. <br /><br />-	<b>There is predictability to the way it ended; also, there is no real closure</b> which obviously causes people to immediately want to get their hands on the second installment; but for me it just wasn't satisfactory or fulfilling.<br /><br />-	<b>The romance part of the book was a huge miss for me too, there was no love here</b>, and since love is such an essential element for me, this lack evidently also influenced my bad rating. <br /><br />That’s just my opinion, I do realize that I am in the minority.</span>

<div id="review_372860926" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/372860926" />
    <a title="Jill" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3820197-jill"><img alt="Jill" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383385041p2/3820197.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/372860926?book_show_action=true">Jul 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jill" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jill" href="/user/show/3820197-jill">Jill</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3820197-jill?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3820197-jill?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer372860926" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2457703080044059092"><br/><b>3.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Sara McMillan becomes enthralled reading a stranger's journal that her neighbour got from a storage sale. The journal belongs to Rebecca Mason and details Rebecca's pull into a darkly erotic and possibly dangerous relationship. Deciding that her possessions and journals should be returned, Sara tries to track down the missing Rebecca. <br/><br/>She finds out that Rebecca works for <i>Allure Art Gallery</i>, San Francisco's largest and most prestigious gallery. But when told that Rebecca is on leave, Sar</span>
  <span id="freeText2457703080044059092" style="display:none"><br /><b>3.5 stars</b><br /><br />Sara McMillan becomes enthralled reading a stranger's journal that her neighbour got from a storage sale. The journal belongs to Rebecca Mason and details Rebecca's pull into a darkly erotic and possibly dangerous relationship. Deciding that her possessions and journals should be returned, Sara tries to track down the missing Rebecca. <br /><br />She finds out that Rebecca works for <i>Allure Art Gallery</i>, San Francisco's largest and most prestigious gallery. But when told that Rebecca is on leave, Sara a high school teacher, offers to fill in at the gallery over her summer break. Since Sara loves art, has an Art degree and has interned at an Art Museum, she's hired. Working at Rebecca's job, Sara may be able to find out more about Rebecca and where she is.<br /><br />Chris Merit is an artist whose work is displayed at <i>Allure</i>. Soon Sara is drawn into a relationship with the artsy rebel, who hints at a dark and twisted past. But she also attracts the attention of Mark Compton, <i>Allure's</i> manager. Both these men are attractive, successful and hiding secrets.<br /><br />This is the first in the <i>Inside Out Trilogy</i>, a combination of romance, erotic themes and mystery. <i>If I Were You</i> has a lot going for it, but by far the mystery was the real drawcard for me. The journals were written with just the right amount of intrigue, suspense and eroticism that had me wanting to know more of this mystery woman, Rebecca Mason. <br /><br />The romance between Sara and Chris didn't work as well. As in a number of romances, I really couldn't see why Chris (who can have his pick of any woman in the world), chooses Sara specifically. Their relationship felt rather abrupt and quick. The 'dark' part of the hero did feel a little contrived, often talking about his dark side, without ever giving any real indication, until near the end of the story where a piece of his disturbing past is revealed.<br /><br />I'm surprised that <i>If I Were You</i> is promoted as <i>Fifty Shades of Grey meets Basic Instinct</i>. Though I've not read <i>FSoG</i> I know enough about it and I couldn't really see the connection, nor with <i>Basic Instinct</i>. However, the author must know what she's doing and perhaps this comes into play more in the next books. Comparing <i>If I Were You</i> to <i>FSoG</i> though could also be seen as a bit dicey and a turnoff for a number of readers. <br /><br /><i>If I Were You</i> is much more akin to <i>Bared to You</i> (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13451045.Bared_to_You__Crossfire___1_" title="Bared to You (Crossfire, #1) by Sylvia Day" rel="nofollow noopener">Bared to You</a>) meets <i>Scandalous</i> (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13602986.Scandalous" title="Scandalous by Ella Steele" rel="nofollow noopener">Scandalous</a>).<br /><br />Where this book has the advantage is in the gripping mystery woven into the story. The journal entries are dark, edgy and hints at some kink and possible danger that Rebecca may have gotten into. Readers are left with some burning questions at the end of this book.<br /><br />Who really is Rebecca Mason, the writer of the journals? Where is she now? Is she really missing? Is her non-appearance (or disappearance) suspicious? Who is the man she refers to in her journals? Could it be Mark? Chris even? Or is it someone else altogether?<br /><br />This was a very difficult novel to rate as certain aspects worked very well, others didn't. So if I could divvy if up like this -<br /><br />Mystery 4.5/5<br />Sex scenes 4/5<br />Writing 3.5/5<br />Plot 3.5/5 <br />Characterisations 3.5/5<br />Hero/heroine 3.5/5<br />Romance 2/5<br /><br />Overall, I'd give it 3.5 stars. I'd recommend it to readers of erotic contemporary romance, readers who enjoyed <i>Bared to You</i> and possibly those who enjoyed <i>FSoG</i>.<br /><br />Kudos Ms Jones for drawing me into this mystery so deftly that despite my lack of enthusiasm for the actual romance, I did find the mystery compelling and enough to draw me into the next book to find out more about Rebecca Mason.<br /><br /><b>Steam:</b> 3.5<br /><br /><br /><i>ARC courtesy of Lisa Renee Jones via NetGalley</i><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2457703080044059092" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2728555343617639224">I know I'm going one amongst the minority when I say this ! But I honestly can't STAND to read another word from this predictable 'mystery-slash-good old erotica' novel anymore :P<br/><br/>No seriously, you're going to have to shoot me.In fact I freakin insist.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/628489.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Honestly, I think I'm quite done with reading books with the exact same concepts.<br/><i>One damaged billionaire?   <span id="freeText2728555343617639224" style="display:none">I know I'm going one amongst the minority when I say this ! But I honestly can't STAND to read another word from this predictable 'mystery-slash-good old erotica' novel anymore :P<br><br>No seriously, you're going to have to shoot me.In fact I freakin insist.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/628489.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Honestly, I think I'm quite done with reading books with the exact same concepts.<br><i>One damaged billionaire?
